# proposal-amendment >> proposal-amendment-book (OpenBookingApprovalFlow >> Multiple)

**Booking Flow:** OpenBookingApprovalFlow

**Opportunity Type:** Multiple

**Feature:** Approval Flow / Proposal Amendment - Amend an opportunity using an OrderProposal (Implemented) 

**Test:**  Successful booking using the Booking Flow with Approval, creating an amendment

A successful end to end booking, via Booking Flow with Approval, of an opportunity, creating an amendment.

### Running only this test

```bash
npm start -- --runInBand test/features/approval/proposal-amendment/implemented/proposal-amendment-book-test.js
```

```json
{
```
```json
  "headers": {
```
